1. goto: https://emojipedia.org/

DONE ==> ClientData stored sorting order!!!!!

bei jedem der folgenden fragt es sich: who is updating fen?

1. singleplayer: 
- only 1 player has turn, all others are polling,
- when player is done others update

2. race:
- multiple players have turn
- all players are polling
- first player who is done, writes
- all update

3. collect:
- multiple players have turn
- all are polling
- when all are done, server notifies complete
- upon completion host gets to update fen
- all update

variants: 
- player can [override] until complete or first entry counts
- player selections are [hidden] or visible as soon as entered

4. timed collect:
- multiple players have turn
- all are polling
- when time is up, server writes
- all update
5. timed race:
- multiple players have turn
- all players are polling
- first player who is done before timeup, writes
- all update
